NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL  NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By  Order)
Director  of  Stationery  and  Printing.

NOTICES
YENPEYESS RUBBER PRIVATE LIMITED
226, MUNDAGA NADAR STREET, SIVAKASI-626 123.
Notice is hereby given to the Public that the Company M/s. YEPEYESS RUBBER PRIVATE LIMITED having registered
office at No. 226, Mundaga Nadar Street, Sivakasi-626 123, has Passed a Special Resolution at the Extraordinay General
Meeting held on 13-12-2012 for Voluntarily liquidating the company as follows:
тRESOLVED THAT pursuant to the provisions of Section 484 (1) (b) of the Companies Act, 1956 and having regard
to the declaration made by the board of directors dated 09-11-2012 and delivered to the Registrar of Companies,
Tamil Nadu, Chennai under Section 488 of the companies Act, 1956 stating that the company would be able to pay its
debts in full within a period not exceeding one year from the date of commencement of winding up, the consent of the
members of the Company, be and is hereby accorded to wind up the affairs of the Company as the membersт voluntary
winding up, with effect from 13-12-2012.т
The above said resolution and connected documents will be filed with the Registrar of Companies, Tamil Nadu,
Chennai in due course.
Chennai,
N. SUDARSANAN,
20th December 2012.
Director.

SALBROS ENGINEERS PRIVATE LIMITED
REGD. OFFICE: 3, 21st CROSS STREET, INDIRA NAGAR, MADRAS-20, TAMIL NADU
Notice is hereby given that, pursuant to Section 485 of the Companies Act, 1956, the Company in terms of
Section 484 (1) (b) of the Companies Act, 1956, passed a Special Resolution at the Extraordinary General Meeting held
on 14th December, 2012 to wind up the Company by members voluntary winding up.
That the Company has appointed Mr. Natarajan Ramamoorthy as Liquidator of the Company for the purpose of such
winding up as per the provisions of the Companies Act, 1956.
Chennai, 20th December 2012.
NATARAJAN RAMAMOORTHY,
Liquidator.
